### B719 — Road curb/border drawn far too thick: size it to a true 6″ (0.5′) curb, to scale `[Site Planner]` (bug) #site-planner #road #ui  *(owner-dropped 2026-07-08 as "NEW-2"; minted **B719** = highest B# across both files (B718) + 1. Branch `claude/road-editing-curb-scale-r1u2sw`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + headless-verified this session; parks in ⏳ Verify (Verify: live — zoom-/data-density-dependent rendering + PDF/print export parity, both mandatory-live classes) → V248.** A road's edge/curb line rendered as a fat pixel band unrelated to real size; it now represents a true **6″ (0.5 US survey ft)** curb, sized `curb × ppf`, so it reads as a thin to-scale line at site zoom and grows proportionally on zoom-in.
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-08 from chat
- **DEDUPE-FIRST:** B70/B71 define the curb *contract* (6″ default / 12″ trailer, three-way draw/calc/dimension rule); B180/B181 cover curb in the *cost/area* takeoff; B601 renders the centerline road surface+curb. None address the render *stroke weight* — this is a pure visual-scale fix, no new number needed elsewhere.
- **Root cause:** the centerline road's pavement edge + curb stripes (and the legacy rect road's) were stroked with `strokeZoom(...)` — a near-constant pixel weight (≈5–7px edge / ≈3px stripe at site zoom), clamped, with no tie to the 6″ curb. A real 6″ curb is `0.5 × ppf` px (sub-pixel at overview zoom), so the strokes read as a fat band many times the true curb.
- **Fix:** new pure `curbStrokePx(curbFt, ppf, minPx)` in `lib/roadGeometry.js` (floored so it stays visible sub-pixel, NO ceiling → proportional on zoom-in). `SitePlanner.jsx` road render: the centerline pavement edge + curb stripes and the legacy rect road's border + stripes now use `curbStrokePx(roadCurbWidth(el), ppf, CURB_STROKE_MIN_PX=0.75)`. No new geometry / data — purely edge styling sized to 6″ (a 12″ trailer curb renders exactly 2× via the same formula). Selection cue stays the blue handles (B619). Export parity holds by construction (`printSheet.js` clones the live SVG).
- **Verified (sandbox/headless):** `test/roadGeometry.test.js` `curbStrokePx` cases (to-scale above floor / floored sub-pixel / non-finite guard) · `test/bugHuntGuards.test.js` new B719 guard (roads use `curbStrokePx`, not `strokeZoom`) · full suite green · lint 0 errors · build green · MAP regenerated. **`ui-audit/verify-b718-b719.mjs` (logged-out, real app): the 6″ curb stripe = 1.03px at fit (vs the old ~3px band) and a 12″ curb road = 2.06px — ratio exactly 2.00, proving stroke = curb × ppf (to scale), not a fixed pixel weight; the road still renders as a filled, legible strip; 0 page errors.**
- **⏳ V248 (live, on planyr.io):** eyeball the thin to-scale curb on a real project at several zooms (and nudge the 0.75px floor up if it reads faint at overview zoom), and confirm the PDF/print export shows the same thin curb (PDF-PARITY — the export clones the live SVG so parity is expected, but this is a mandatory-live class).

### B734 — Account dropdown opens pinned to the top-left corner instead of under the account pill `[App Shell / UI]` (bug) #ui #infra  *(owner-dropped 2026-07-09 as "NEW-1"; **B734** = highest B# across both files (B733) + 1. Branch `claude/account-menu-positioning-frp60c`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + sandbox/headless-verified this session; parks in ⏳ Verify (Verify: live — the account dropdown is signed-in-only and the sandbox can't sign in) → V250.** Clicking the signed-in account pill ("Michael Butler" + avatar) at the header's top-right opened its dropdown (Profile / Team / Settings / Sign out) pinned to the **top-left corner** of the viewport; it now drops straight down under the pill, right-aligned, staying inside the screen edge.
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-09 from chat
- **DEDUPE-FIRST:** searched Open / ⏳ Verify / Done (BACKLOG*.md + BACKLOG_OPEN.md) — **net-new**, no existing item covers the account/user/profile dropdown position. Nearest prior art to BUILD ON, NOT a dupe: **B127** (Done — built `src/shared/ui/AnchoredMenu.jsx`, the portal-to-body rect-anchored menu the account dropdown already uses; that bug was menus *clipped/behind* the rail, a different symptom). Account-name/identity-pill work (B297/B298) is the pill itself, not its menu position.
- **AUDIT-FIRST — the report's guess was wrong.** The report suspected a missing `position`/lost `position:relative`. Neither: `AnchoredMenu`'s math and the account menu's `placement="below-right"` were already correct. **Real cause:** Shell built ONE `authControl` element (with a single `acctAnchor` ref + `<AnchoredMenu>`) and the keep-alive render (2026-07-05) passes that SAME element into **every visited workspace's `AppHeader`** — up to 5 mount at once (Site map header + Site plan header + DocReview + Library + Scheduler), most `display:none`. All the button copies shared one `acctAnchor`, so `acctAnchor.current` resolved to whichever copy React committed last — usually a hidden one. `getBoundingClientRect()` on a `display:none` element is all-zeros, so `below-right` (`left = a.right - mw`) went negative → clamped to (8px, 8px) = top-left. Explains why it was fine on a fresh load but broke after switching workspaces/modes once. Every OTHER `AnchoredMenu` consumer already creates its anchor ref *locally inside its own component* (e.g. `SettingsMenu`, `ProjectBreadcrumb`) — so it never had this bug.
- **Fix:** extracted the whole auth surface into a self-contained **`src/app/AccountControl.jsx`** (own `acctAnchor` ref + `acctOpen`/`cloudNote` state per instance). Passing the same `<AccountControl/>` element to multiple `{authControl}` slots creates an INDEPENDENT component instance (independent hooks) at each fiber position, so each mounted header anchors to its OWN visible button and only the clicked one opens — the SettingsMenu/ProjectBreadcrumb pattern (MODULE-SCOPE-COMPONENTS). Shell now just builds `<AccountControl user profileApi onOpenAuth onOpenAccount />` and keeps driving the `AuthPanel` modal; no workspace forwarder or `AppHeader` changed. Secondary class-wide hardening: lifted `AnchoredMenu`'s placement math into pure, unit-tested **`src/shared/ui/anchoredMenuPlacement.js` (`placeMenu`)**, which returns `null` for a zero-sized anchor so a mis-anchored menu stays *hidden* instead of pinning to the corner (all three placements — `left`/`below-left`/`below-right` — preserved, so no other consumer regresses).
- **Verified (sandbox/headless):** new `test/anchoredMenuPlacement.test.js` (8 cases — below-right/below-left/left anchoring, right/bottom/left clamps, zero-rect → null, missing → null) · B557 account-email null-guard test repointed to `AccountControl.jsx` (the guard rode with the code) · full unit suite green (3147) · lint 0 errors · build green · MAP.md + shared folder-pointer regenerated. Headless logged-out smoke: app boots clean, no stray menu at the corner, and another `AnchoredMenu` consumer still positions correctly (the shared-`placeMenu` refactor didn't regress it).
- **⏳ V250 (live, on planyr.io, SIGNED IN — the sandbox can't sign in):** open the account pill → menu drops directly under it, right-aligned, fully on-screen; switch workspaces/modes and reopen → still anchored under the pill (never top-left, no duplicate/stacked menus); Esc + click-outside still dismiss.

- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-08 from chat

FAST PATH returns the exact additive sum when there are 0/1 valid rings or NO overlapping pair (`overlappingParcelPairs` empty — adjacent lots share only an edge), so every normal, non-overlapping site is byte-identical to the old number (no rounding jitter); clipper runs only on genuine overlap. B652 warning copy updated (area is now correct — the warning flags the duplicate to review, no longer claims inflation).

### B707 — Floodplain mitigation engine: rules matrix + elevation-based compensating-storage volume `[Site Planner / Stormwater]` (feature) #site-planner #gis #pond  *(owner consolidated brief 2026-07-07, arrived as "NEW-1" — absorbs the earlier mitigation-engine draft + its rev-2 elevation core + the WSE/AO-AH amendment; minted **B707** = highest real B# across both files (B706) + 1 — the B3340/B5263/B25431 grep hits in BACKLOG-DONE.md are CSS hex colours, not IDs. Copy notes jurisdictions may enforce newer model elevations than the effective FIRM — when in doubt enter the higher.

- **What shipped:** `layerRequest.imageLayerOptions` passes an OBJECT `cfg.rendering` through verbatim as the whole `renderingRule` (string configs unchanged); `TERRAIN.elevation` carries the measured chain, plain-language label **"Ground relief (low = blue, high = red)"**, `source: USGS 3DEP`, and a note that colors are **RELATIVE TO THE CURRENT VIEW** (DRA re-shuffles on pan — without the note that reads as a bug), NAVD88, screening-only. ### B704 — 1-ft labeled contour lines, client-generated from the raw 3DEP DEM in a Web Worker `[Site Planner / GIS]` (feature) #site-planner #gis #perf  *(owner brief 2026-07-07, arrived as "NEW-2"; **B704** = B703 + 1. Branch `claude/elevation-houston-relief-7co7do`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + headless-verified this session; parks (Verify: live — GIS endpoint + zoom-/data-density-dependent rendering classes) → V240.**
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-07 from chat
- **Why client-side:** the public service's canned contour renderings are raster-only, unlabeled, and (at best preset) 2-ft — no labeled 1-ft vector lines exist server-side. The raw grid path was probe-verified first: `exportImage?format=lerc&pixelType=F32&renderingRule=None` returns LERC1 (`CntZImage`), decoded with the official `lerc` npm package; a real Katy tile is committed as `test/fixtures/dep-katy-463x400.lerc` (463×400 F32, 120.9–149.8 ft — drives the decode-contract tests without network).
- **What shipped (new deps: `lerc` + `d3-contour`, both small — the two the brief authorized):**
  - **Pure core** (`lib/demGrid.js`, `lib/contours.js`): deterministic snapped-tile grid requests (key ↔ bbox bijection; smoothing margin baked in; oversized viewports coarsen deterministically; `adjustAspectRatio=false` + size computed to match the bbox aspect exactly — a silently adjusted bbox would shift every contour, and a size mismatch on decode REFUSES loudly); LERC magic-byte sniff (the dev server SPA-fallbacks `/api/*` to index.html — "response arrived" ≠ "response is a grid"); meters → survey-ft on decode (`M_TO_FT` now exported from `elevation.js` — one conversion for every 3DEP consumer); normalized MASKED gaussian smooth (voids never bleed; unsmoothed 1-ft contours from ±0.1–0.3 ft LiDAR noise are jagged spaghetti); marching squares via `d3-contour` with **sentinel-embedded voids** (never NaN — d3's smoothing emits NaN coords and Leaflet throws) and **two strip passes** (grid-border frame + dilated-void halo, so lines BREAK at water instead of bridging or outlining it); pixel-space Douglas–Peucker (the newly exported `vectorLayers.douglasPeucker`; degree-space tolerance is anisotropic on the ground); index flag every 5 ft; sparse labels capped ~30.
  - **The repo's first Web Worker** (`lib/terrainWorker.js`, Vite `?worker`): decode/smooth/trace off the main thread; import list pinned by `test/terrainWorker.test.js` (a Leaflet/DOM import would crash at worker RUNTIME, not build time); the raw grid transfers back for the B706 readout.
  - **Leaflet glue** (`lib/terrainLayers.js`): overpass-pattern view-driven layerGroup (moveend refresh, B56d busy/pending trailing edge, `gisCache.swr` last-good painting with data age) with the terrain specifics — fetch on the MAIN thread (gisCache is localStorage-bound; proxy→direct one-shot fallback mirrors wireRaster), ONE deduped fetch+compute per tile shared with B705 and the readout, grids in a small LRU Map (a Float32Array must never ride `gisCache.write` — it JSON.stringifies unconditionally), canvas-renderer polylines (`interactive:false`; hierarchy by WEIGHT per the salience rule), white-halo divIcon labels, restyle-in-place `setOpacity`, worker-crash lazy rebuild.
  - **Registry** (`lib/layers.js`): `TERRAIN.contours` ("Contour lines (1 ft)"), `kind: "contours"` dispatch, vintage row; both surfaces pick it up automatically. **Zoom-gated ≥ 16** (honesty: at z15 a capped grid is ~6 m cells — 1-ft contours would be mush).
  - **Calibration:** the ramp test pins d3-contour's smoothed output to the cell-center convention (measured: level 20 of an x-ramp lands at exactly px 20.5), so contours, the hover readout, and the cross-section tool can never disagree by half a cell. Elevations are NAVD88 orthometric — the same vertical datum FEMA BFEs use (stated in the layer note; relevant to the future FFE-vs-BFE feature).
- **Verified here (sandbox):** 60+ new unit tests across the `demGrid`/`contours`/`terrainWorker` suites (calibration, cone closed-ring, void break-not-bridge with halo assertion, masked-smooth void-bleed, fixture decode contract, artifact under the 512 KB cache cap) · full suite green · build green (worker chunk emits self-contained) · headless: ONE LERC fetch, 30 halo labels painted, real canvas ink, vintage + caveat lines render.
> **Dedup (DEDUPE-FIRST — grepped contour / DEM / topo / LERC across Open/⏳/Done):** B691 (Open) = the Fort Bend COUNTY contour GIS layer (different source, CORS/proxy plumbing — untouched); B497/B500 (Done) = pond stage contours (detention geometry, not terrain); B58/B23 (Done) = the getSamples profile path whose conventions this reuses. Client-generated terrain contours are net-new.

### B705 — Drainage flow-direction arrows (which way the site sheets) `[Site Planner / GIS]` (feature) #site-planner #gis  *(owner brief 2026-07-07, arrived as "NEW-3"; **B705** = B704 + 1. Branch `claude/elevation-houston-relief-7co7do`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + headless-verified this session; parks (Verify: live — zoom-/data-density class) → V241.**
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-07 from chat
- **What shipped:** `lib/flowField.js` (pure): downhill direction from a central-difference **gradient** over the harder-smoothed grid, windowed to the sample spacing — raw per-cell D8 at sparse samples reads as random 8-quantized noise on near-flat Houston terrain, so the gradient drives the ARROWS while **classic D8 is kept alongside, pure, as the seed of the future storm-outfall flow-accumulation feature** (extend D8 → accumulation to answer "which outfall does this part of the site drain to" — the B641-adjacent note the brief asked recorded). Screen-spaced lattice (~70 px); arrow length + weight scale with slope (bolder = steeper — salience tracks importance); slope computed in ft/ft with the cos(lat) mercator→ground correction (~0.868 at Houston — mercator meters overstate ground distance ~15%). **Flat/ambiguous/void samples get NO arrow** — never invent a direction (the no-auto-guess principle). Rides B704's tile end-to-end: NO second DEM fetch path (the same worker job computes both artifacts). Sign-convention unit tests pin east-falling → east arrows and south-falling → down-screen arrows (grid y-down vs latitude-up is the classic silent bug — uphill arrows pass every other test).
- **Verified here (sandbox):** flowField unit suite (sign pins, ground-meter slope, flat → no arrows, void suppression, lattice spacing) · headless: toggling Drainage direction after Contours fires ZERO additional grid fetches, arrows add real canvas ink, and on the real Katy tile the arrows visibly point INTO the channel depression crossing the view (screenshot) — physically coherent on real data.
> **Dedup (DEDUPE-FIRST — grepped drainage / flow / arrow / outfall across Open/⏳/Done):** B641 (Later) = outfall flowline/tailwater SOURCING; B636–B639 (Done) = regulatory/hydraulic drainage rules. No existing item draws DEM-derived flow direction on the map. Net-new.

### B706 — Hover ground-elevation readout on the cursor coordinate chips `[Site Planner]` (feature) #site-planner #gis #ui  *(owner brief 2026-07-07, arrived as "NEW-4"; **B706** = B705 + 1. Branch `claude/elevation-houston-relief-7co7do`.)*

- Origin: filed 2026-07-07 from chat
- **What shipped:** both B683 coordinate chips (map finder bottom-center; planner bottom-left) append **"· El ≈ 132.3 ft NAVD88"** at the cursor. New `components/useGroundElevation.js` hook: with a terrain-layer grid covering the view it bilinear-samples locally on every move (instant, zero network — the **UNSMOOTHED** grid, so it agrees with the cross-section tool, not the smoothed cartography); otherwise ONE debounced (~300 ms cursor-rest) `elevation.samplePoint` getSamples call — never per-mousemove. Superseded requests abort; a result is tied to the position it was asked for (a slow response can never paint a stale number under a new position). **No-data/void/failure all render as ABSENCE** — the segment simply doesn't appear (a confident number over water would be a lie). Screening caveat rides the chip's `title`. The planner chip now reprojects through one shared memo (same `feetToLatLng`, display unchanged).

### B699 — Whole content pane is the drop target; drag-onto-folder files into it; ONE empty state; folder drops preserve your subfolder structure `[Library / storage]` (feature) #library #files #filing #drive  *(owner brief 2026-07-07, arrived as "NEW-3"; **B699** = B698 + 1. Branch `claude/library-tab-refactor-suqn3m`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED this session; parks in ⏳ Verify (Verify: live — drag-and-drop is the timing/race class, and filing into arbitrary Drive folders is live-Drive behavior) → V237.** Explorer model throughout.
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-07 from chat
- RENUMBERED on merge-in of `origin/main` 2026-07-07 — concurrent sessions took B689–B696 (basemap/boundary-layers batch, husk root-cause, de-creams, CORS proxy) and V232–V235; this branch's B689–B694 / V232–V234 became **B697–B702 / V236–V238** (= highest across both files + 1). Code comments were bumped to match.
- **What shipped:**
  - The **whole pane is the drop target**, driven by a dragenter/dragleave **depth counter** (the old naive `currentTarget === target` dragleave flickered over children — the exact gotcha the brief flagged).
  - **Drag onto a folder row** in the left rail highlights it (dashed accent) and drops file straight into that folder; the "All files" row is the drop-to-auto-sort target; the drop-overlay pill names the REAL target (hovered row > selected folder > auto-file).
  - The dedicated bottom **drop card is gone**, and so is the duplicate "No files here yet…" line — ONE empty state ("Drop files anywhere. PDFs read their own title block and file themselves; anything uncertain lands in Needs filing." + Choose files / Choose a folder). Persistent pickers moved to the toolbar (Upload files / Upload a folder).
  - **Structure preservation (decision baked into the brief):** a dropped/picked FOLDER routes each file by the user's own SUBFOLDER layout — a subfolder matching an existing tree folder files straight into it (prefix/case-insensitive, plural-tolerant; `matchDropPathToFolder` in `shared/folders/folderTree.js`, unit-tested); a subfolder matching nothing goes to **Needs filing** (the tree is never auto-extended). **The dropped CONTAINER's own name never routes anything** (a generic "Drawings"/"Documents" container must not mass-file by coincidence) — its direct files keep the classic B664 title-block auto-file, so a plain folder of PDFs never dumps on Needs filing. **Never-guess guards:** an ambiguous label is accepted only when its parent segment pins exactly one candidate; a unique label reached through a CONTRADICTING known parent ("Design/Reports" where the only "Reports" folder lives under Testing Contractor) is rejected and the walk files into the nearest corroborated ancestor (Design) instead — cross-branch guessing is structurally impossible. An explicit target (row drop / selected folder) still wins for the whole drop (B686/B687 semantics); a drop before the tree rows load falls back to classic auto-file (no empty-tree needs-filing dump); a drag cancelled outside the window resets the pane highlight (window dragend/drop/leave self-heal); rail navigation and the queue's Triage button clear an active search so a click never looks dead. The entry-API walk now stamps `relPath` (`uploadQueue.entryToFiles`); `webkitdirectory` picks already carry `webkitRelativePath`. All ingestion still rides the ONE B260-descended queue (`makeQueueItems`/`runPool`) — no forked pipeline; the folder-note summary honestly reports kept / needs-filing / skipped counts.
- **Verified here (sandbox):** unit tests (path-matcher ambiguity + contradiction rules, relPath stamping) · full suite green · build green · logged-out headless smoke.
- **🔍 Adversarially reviewed (2026-07-07, 4 dimensions × verify): confirmed findings all fixed same-session** — the cross-branch unique-label guess (HIGH → the contradiction guard above), the container-name mass-file (container excluded from routing), a LOWERCASED folder label stamped as the discipline corrupting doc-class/category (labels now case-preserved + normalized onto the canonical discipline list), row-hop highlight flicker (targets now arm on dragenter), a depth-counter desync pinning the overlay after an out-of-window release (window-dragleave self-heal), the folderRows-empty race, over-promising drop copy (the empty state + overlay pill now name the REAL target), and dead-feeling clicks with a search active (rail clicks / Triage clear the query; typing exits the holding view).
> **Dedup (DEDUPE-FIRST — grepped `drop` / `drag` / `entry` / `empty state` across Open/⏳/Done):** extends **B664** (folder drops — the flatten-and-file source side) and **B687** (selected-folder targeting) with row-targeted drops + structure preservation; neither covered them. The B686/B687 folder-pick-wins rule is preserved unchanged.

### B701 — Honest Drive-sync footer: backend-driven resting status, "Synced · N min ago", loud failure `[Library / storage]` (bug — silent-failure class) #library #drive #persistence  *(owner brief 2026-07-07, arrived as "NEW-6"; **B701** = B700 + 1. Branch `claude/library-tab-refactor-suqn3m`.)*

- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-07 from chat
- RENUMBERED on merge-in of `origin/main` 2026-07-07 — concurrent sessions took B689–B696 (basemap/boundary-layers batch, husk root-cause, de-creams, CORS proxy) and V232–V235; this branch's B689–B694 / V232–V234 became **B697–B702 / V236–V238** (= highest across both files + 1). Code comments were bumped to match.
- **AUDIT-FIRST (brief vs code — the brief's worst fear didn't hold):** the ✓ was NOT a static label — `DriveBadge` was already driven by the real `syncFoldersToDrive` result (`ok`/`skipped`→off/`error`, error already red + Retry). The REAL gaps: no timestamp (so "Mirrored ✓" beside "Sync now" read as a contradiction), no RESTING status (state was per-session `useState` — a mirrored-but-untouched project showed NOTHING at rest, and a project switch could inherit the previous project's status), and the ✓ glyph was a catch-all default rather than gated to `ok`. Also stale: the brief's "B207 Drive backend still blocked on OAuth" — Drive has been live since 2026-06-22; the `off` state remains the honest not-connected rendering.
- **What shipped:** `ok` → "✓ Synced to Google Drive · N min ago" (ticking via `relTime`); the last CONFIRMED sync per project persists (`planyr:library:driveSyncAt:v1:<pid>`) and restores at mount ONLY when every live folder already carries its Drive id (the mount reconcile then re-verifies against the real backend within seconds); `off` → amber "Saved in Planyr — Google Drive isn't connected."; `error` → red persistent + Retry (unchanged); ✓ strictly the ok glyph; project switches reset the footer. **"Sync now" demoted** to a quiet tertiary link with explicit semantics (title: forces a full reconcile — every folder re-checked, anything missing re-mirrored). Follows the B125 honest-badge rules on the existing `{ok/skipped/error}` contract — no parallel status system.
> **Dedup:** hardens B650/B662's own badge (their `{ok:false}`-contract work is reused wholesale); the B125 save badge is the pattern model, reused not duplicated.

### B694 — County / city / ETJ boundary layers ride the cached vector tier: instant paint, no 503 stalls `[Site Planner / GIS]` (feature — amends B96, touches B176/B287) #site-planner #gis #perf  *(owner brief 2026-07-07, arrived as "NEW-2"; minted **B694**. `[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + headless-verified this session; parks (Verify: live — GIS endpoint behavior is a mandatory live class; the sandbox egress proxy RESETS browser connections to services.arcgis.com, so the live pull can only be confirmed on planyr.io) → V234.**
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-07 from chat
- RENUMBERED on merge-in of `origin/main` 2026-07-07 — concurrent sessions took B693 (left-menu de-cream) + B694 (husk-parcel render guard) + B695 (Fort Bend contours CORS proxy) + B696 (husk root-cause) and V233; this branch's B693–B696 / V233–V235 became **B693–B696 / V234–V235** (= highest across both files + 1). Code comments were bumped to match.
- **AUDIT-FIRST correction to the brief:** the brief said the vector tier "already shipped for FEMA/NWI" — in fact `lib/vectorLayers.js` was UNWIRED groundwork (its only consumer was its own test; the earlier `vectorOverlay.js` had been deleted as unwired, and FEMA/NWI render via the raster f=image path to this day). This session built the tier's **first live consumer**. ⚠ Standing discrepancy left in place: `VECTOR_SOURCES.wetlands.query.url` still points at the dead `fwspublicservices` host (dormant row, no runtime consumer — repoint it if/when NWI vectors get wired).
- **What shipped:** `jur_county` / `jur_city` / `jur_etj` flip `kind:"esriFeature"` → **`kind:"vector"`** and render through the new **`lib/vectorOverlay.js`** (`cachedVectorLayer`): paint the last-good copy from the browser SWR cache (B96 `gisCache`) instantly, refresh in the background, swap fresh geometry in via a new `fetchCached onFresh` passthrough, and report `{ts, stale}` so the panel shows the copy's age. Engine additions (`lib/vectorLayers.js`, all pure + unit-tested): **detail tiers** (`pickTier`) with **server-side generalization** (`maxAllowableOffset` — the agency thins vertices before the wire, replacing client Douglas–Peucker for tiered pulls, which is the brief's per-zoom simplify done cheaper), tier-stamped cache keys (`vectorKey`), and **outward grid-snap** (`snapBbox`) so pans reuse entries.
- **Cache design (measured live 2026-07-07 via curl):** county coarse tier = ONE statewide source-level entry (`vec:jur_county:all@0.002`, 254 counties, **337 KB** @0.002° ≈ 200 m — fits the 512 KB `maxEntryBytes` cap, so no per-county split; the brief's open question, answered empirically); ETJ coarse = one H-GAC-region entry (608 features, **204 KB** @0.001°); city is always bbox-scoped (statewide too heavy; a metro cell ≈ **120 KB**). Fine tiers (z≥12/13) are bbox-scoped @0.0002° on a snap grid. TTLs: county 30 d, city/ETJ 14 d (annexations/SB2038 move these occasionally; SWR shows age either way). Per B96's own note, the **refreshed-age stamp folded into the B236 vintage line** — one surface: `as of: <vintage> · refreshed <age> (updating…)`, stale in `--warn-text` (the standalone age chip is gone).
- **Never-blank fallback (the decideVectorOrImage intent, adapted):** boundaries are always-vector (no image service exists) — `minVectorZoom:0`/`maxAreaDeg:∞` so no gate can flip them; a **failed pull with nothing cached** engages the injected live fallback = the previous esri-leaflet `featureLayer` path **with its B287 retry/backoff**, LOUD through the same status channel (`liveFallback`, dependency-injected from `layers.js` so `vectorOverlay` stays esri-leaflet-free). A cold-cache fetch failure now THROWS in `fetchCached` instead of resolving a silent null (LOUD-FAILURE). B176 invariant preserved: same `GIS_SOURCES` endpoints as the jurisdiction identify — the line you see is the line the identify reports.
- **Verified here (sandbox):** 48 vectorLayers unit tests (tiers/snap/keys/onFresh/cold-throw/registry) + headless with a seeded cache + the TxDOT host BLOCKED: boundaries painted in **~50 ms with zero network**, one statewide cache entry (`vec:jur_county:all@0.002p4`), folded age line rendering, toggle-off clears clean, zero page errors. The correctly-shaped statewide query (no envelope + `maxAllowableOffset=0.002`) observed leaving the browser before the sandbox proxy reset it — the live leg is V234.
- **🔍 Adversarially reviewed (2026-07-07, 4 dimensions; verify agents hit the session token cap so every finding was verified BY HAND against the code): 18 raw findings → 10 root causes confirmed, all fixed same-session.** The theme: the overlay's race guards and the fallback's honesty. Fixed: (1) `engageFallback` + the zoom-gate branch now bump the request `seq` — an in-flight fetch can no longer paint stale vectors OVER the live fallback or BELOW the zoom gate; (2) a SUPERSEDED request's failure no longer latches `lastVectorError` (and a successful pull clears it) — a mid-pan blip can't permanently downgrade the layer to the fallback; (3) the fallback layer gets the `setOpacity` shim esri-leaflet FeatureLayers lack (the opacity slider was dead after engagement) and reports "loading", not a false-healthy "loaded", right after the failure that engaged it; (4) the basemap status dot keys off `tileload` — Leaflet fires layer-`load` even when EVERY tile errored, which showed green over a gray canvas; (5) a DFW-scale city cell measured **560 KB stored** (over the 512 KB cap → silent L1-only) — the widest city tier now thins at 0.003°/3 dp with a mid tier at z11–12; (6) cache keys stamp `precision` too (`@0.002p4`) so a registry retune busts the cache instead of serving old-detail geometry for a TTL; (7) the identify popover closes on toggle-off/fallback (it used to outlive the layer); (8) a FAILED background refresh clears `lastKey` so the next map move retries (was: "(updating…)" forever with no retry); (9) cold pulls no longer paint twice (swr's cold-fetch `onFresh` is skipped via the `lastKey` guard); (10) select mode neutralizes the interactive fill's `cursor:pointer` (`.pf-select-mode` + `pf-boundary-hit`, index.css) so the +/− parcel cursor survives — B98 extends to the cursor. **Accepted as documented limitations:** gisCache's oldest-write-first eviction could recycle the standing statewide entry under a full 3 MB namespace (a later re-pull, not a failure — changing B96's shared eviction policy would touch the identify/overpass consumers), and an over-cap entry staying L1-only is graceful degradation by design.
> **Dedup:** consumes B96's cache exactly as it anticipated; keeps B287's retry as the fallback leg; does NOT collide with B371 (analysis-side offline pre-cache, still Later) or B629 (parcels).

### B692 — ROOT-CAUSE fix for the B690 husk-parcel crash: sanitize the model funnel so a null/points-less entry can never be manufactured, persisted, or re-ingested `[Site Planner / model]` (bug — CRITICAL, owner-reported crash; extends B690) #site-planner #persistence  *(owner chat 2026-07-07 — incognito tab on planyr.io: "Site Planyr hit an error and couldn't load… Try again/Reload/Ctrl-Shift-R all send me right back." First minted **B689**; RENUMBERED to **B692** on merge-in of `origin/main` — the concurrent Cowork live run independently hit the SAME crash as its V231 #18, minted **B690** for it and shipped the render-side guard (shoelace/polyArea, PR #540), and also took B689 (inspector de-cream) + B691 (Fort Bend CORS); **B692** = highest B# across both files (B691) + 1. Branch `claude/site-planner-incognito-error-49h3as`. DEDUPE-FIRST — same crash as **B690** (both symbolicated to `ym→Hp→Ij`), so this item is deliberately the ROOT-CAUSE COMPANION, not a duplicate: B690 guarded the reads; B692 stops the husk from ever existing — manufacture (normalizeZ), persistence (createSiteModel funnel), and every ingress (rows, realtime, JSON import) — and makes sanitization LOUD.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + fully repro'd/verified headless this session; parks in ⏳ Verify (Verify: live — the repro cites the owner's real signed-in data; the signed-in mirror path + the telemetry signal need a live confirmation) → V232.**
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-07 from chat (crash 2026-07-07 02:23–02:30 UTC, 23 telemetry reports, build dca4f15, all signed-in)
- **Root cause (found via the app's own `client_errors` telemetry — minified stack symbolicated against the deployed chunk):** `MapFinder.siteAcres` reduces `shoelace(p.points)` over `site.parcels`, guarded on the ARRAY but not the ENTRY. A `null` entry in a persisted parcels array (JSON.stringify turns an `undefined` entry or an array hole into `null`) survived `createSiteModel` untouched, and B671's `normalizeZ` then spread it into a `{z:0}` "husk" with no points — `undefined.length` → the workspace error boundary, on EVERY load, because the poison lives in the stored record. Cloud DB swept clean (site_elements + sites blobs, all users) — the husk was client-manufactured into the local mirror during the element-sync churn window (RLS-rejected commit 01:30 + create collisions + a two-tab CAS heal loop 01:33–02:03).
- **Fix (funnel + belt-and-suspenders):** (1) `createSiteModel` now DROPS non-object entries from every collection (parcels/els/markups/measures/callouts/sheetOverlays/parcelDrawings/crossSections) and drops points-less husk parcels — reference-stable when clean, so no state/save churn; runs before `migrateRoads` so a null can't crash the els migration passes either. (2) `normalizeZ`/`needsZ` never spread a non-object into a `{z}` husk (drop instead). (3) `MapFinder.shoelace` returns 0 for a non-array (the list can never crash on residual junk). (4) The rows-read paths (`refetchReplace` + realtime `applyRemoteInstr`) keep husk parcel rows OFF the canvas; the reconcile diff then tombstones the bad row in the cloud — the husk heals into a proper delete (TOMBSTONE-DELETES). (4b) The JSON-import path now normalizes through `createSiteModel` (was raw `setParcels(d.parcels)`) — a hand-edited/stale export can't re-poison the canvas (found by the parallel writer-hunt audit; the audit also confirmed via DB sweep that NO other user has husk data and no one else was affected). (5) LOUD-FAILURE: `loadSitesList` reports a `model-sanitized` telemetry event whenever a stored record needed junk dropped — corruption is a visible signal, never a quiet edit. Bonus: the e2e fixture generator's parcel used `ring:` instead of `points:` (a real husk shipping in the fixture) — fixed + fixtures/goldens regenerated.
- **Self-heal:** no user action — the poisoned record reads clean on the next load (drop-at-read), and the next save persists the cleaned model.
- **Tests/verify (sandbox):** 2,875 green (11 new in `test/modelSanitize.test.js`: husk manufacture, per-collection drops, reference stability, idempotence, junk counting) · build green · **controlled repro BOTH ways headless (`ui-audit/verify-husk-parcel.mjs`): the poisoned seed CRASHES live planyr.io with the owner's exact error, and renders clean (site listed, correct 23.0 ac from the surviving parcel) on the fixed build.**

### B685 — Library upload was PDF-only; accept ANY file type `[Library / Doc Review]` (bug) #library #files #filing #doc-review  *(owner chat 2026-07-06 — "it doesn't let me upload non pdfs, i should be able to upload any file type." **B685** = highest B# across both files (B684) + 1. - Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-06 from chat
- **Root cause:** `isAcceptedFile` (`shared/files/uploadQueue.js`) gated on `application/pdf` / `.pdf`; the `<input accept="application/pdf">` also hid non-PDFs in the OS picker; `partitionAccepted` skipped every non-PDF in folder drops.

Copy generalized ("Choose files", "any file type is welcome", etc.).
- **PDFs keep their powers:** title-block auto-filing + sheet stitching still run for PDFs only (`processItem` skips the title-block read for non-PDFs so pdf.js never chokes on a DWG). A non-PDF inside a project is FILED as "Other" (visible in the tree, re-file anytime) rather than dumped into Needs-filing; cross-project (no project) it still needs a home.

### B684 — Export to Google Earth (KMZ) via right-click, in both the map viewer and the canvas `[Site Planner / Map]` (feature) #site-planner #export #coordinates  *(owner brief 2026-07-06, arrived as "NEW-2"; minted **B684** = B683 + 1. Branch `claude/hopeful-fermi-3yaqcj`. DEDUPE-FIRST — grepped Open/⏳ Verify/Done + BACKLOG-DONE for `kml`/`kmz`/`google earth`/`4326`/`WGS84`: no prior KML/Earth item. Net-new.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + sandbox+headless-verified this session; parks in ⏳ Verify (Verify: live — export parity is a mandatory-LIVE class; the residual is eyeballing registration + 3D massing in the ACTUAL Google Earth app, which the sandbox has no Earth client for) → V226.** Right-click "Export to Google Earth (KMZ)" (+ "Export with 3D buildings") on both the map viewer and the site-planner canvas.
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-06 from chat
- **New pure module `lib/kmzExport.js`** (+ `test/kmzExport.test.js`, 27 tests): dependency-free CRC32 + hand-rolled STORE-only ZIP writer (mirrors `imagePdf.js` — no JSZip), a KML builder, and the site→layer feature mapping. Reprojection is INJECTED (the shared `feetToLatLng`, the SAME transform B683 reuses) so the export can never drift from the map render — one projection path, not two.
- **Reprojection (core requirement):** every foot vertex → WGS84; KML/KMZ is spec'd WGS84. `#1 gotcha` — KML coordinate order is **lon,lat,alt** (reverse of Leaflet's [lat,lng]); the projector flips the pair and a regression test asserts lon-before-lat. A NaN/misregistered projection is treated as crash-severity (LOUD-FAILURE, below).
- **Layers → geometry:** active parcels → Boundary (outline, no fill); buildings / parking / trailer / paving / pond / road / sidewalk / landscape → `<Polygon>` in a per-type folder (fill colors carried from the plan style); centerline roads export their true pavement STRIP (buffered centerline); dock doors → `<Point>` markers; dimension lines → `<LineString>` (optional, default off). Rings auto-closed (first vertex = last); `<innerBoundaryIs>` holes supported at the format layer; placemark `<name>` from the layer label / building number / parcel address.
- **3D massing (enhancement):** "Export with 3D buildings" extrudes each building to its clear height (`<extrude>1</extrude>` + `relativeToGround` + per-vertex altitude in metres); flat `clampToGround` is the default and the fallback when height is unknown.
- **LOUD-FAILURE:** `siteToFeatures` THROWS if any vertex reprojects to a non-finite number → the caller (`flashWarn` on the canvas, `setErr` on the map) aborts loudly, never a partial/misregistered file. Empty site → "nothing to export" (no empty file); a plan with no geo anchor → blocked with a plain-English hint. Names XML-escaped; download filename sanitized. Local download only (default-private; no sharing surface).
- **Two entry points:** map viewer right-click on empty map → exports every visible site (honoring the status-chip filter), each as its own folder, + any selected parcels; canvas right-click on empty space → exports the open plan.
- **Verified (headless, logged-out):** both entry points download a valid `.kmz`; unzipped `doc.kml` is real KML with lon,lat coords near the seeded site (lon=-95.831, lat=29.787), boundary + "Building 1" present. (`gis-verify/kmz-gps-verify.mjs`, 13/13.) Unit: 27 tests (CRC32 vector, ZIP signatures, coordinate order, ring closure, holes, XML escape, NaN guard, extrude toggle, layer mapping, dock-door points, filename). Full suite green · lint 0 errors · build green.
- **⏳ V226** = open a produced `.kmz` in the REAL Google Earth (web or desktop) and confirm: the site lands exactly on the aerial (no lon/lat swap or offset), the layer folders read sensibly, and "Export with 3D buildings" extrudes to a believable height.

### B682 — Dragging a parcel's acreage label spawns a "bunch of copies" (id-less parcels + value-based union merge) `[Site Planner]` (bug) #site-planner #persistence #selection  *(owner chat 2026-07-06 — screenshot: "I just tried to move the 69.48 ac label, and it just made a bunch of copies." **B682** = highest real B# across both files (B681) + 1. Branch `claude/acre-label-duplication-ulvjys`. DEDUPE-FIRST — grepped Open/⏳ Verify/Done for `acre`/`label`/`parcel` × `dup`/`copies`: NOT B651 (split double-COUNTS acreage in the yield math — different defect, same area), NOT B22 (rapid-click duplicate SELECTION on the map). Net-new: the parcel-identity/merge defect.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + sandbox-verified + headless-verified this session; parks in ⏳ Verify (Verify: live — the accumulation is a concurrency/multi-writer MERGE class per LIVE-VERIFY, only fully exercised signed-in over cloud sync) → V225.**
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-06 from chat
- **AUDIT-FIRST root cause:** map-finder / legacy parcels can be **id-LESS**. `MapFinder.computeAssembly` emits `{points, addr, acct, attrs}` with **no `id`** (the modern `newSiteFromMap` backfills one, but records created before that — or synced from an older client — still hold id-less parcels). Two bugs flow from a missing id: (1) the acreage-chip drag matches `pc.id === draggedId`, and with both `undefined` it moves EVERY id-less parcel at once; (2) the cross-copy union merge (`mergeSiteContent` → `unionById`) can only dedupe id-less items by **`JSON.stringify` value**, so the instant a drag adds a `labelOffset` the edited copy no longer equals its stored twin and the union keeps **BOTH** — a phantom parcel that **multiplies** with each further drag/merge. Proven with a focused `mergeSiteContent` repro (1 id-less parcel + a labelOffset edit → **2** parcels).
- **Fix (one funnel, additive):** `createSiteModel` — which every load/save/merge passes through — now backfills a **deterministic id derived from the parcel GEOMETRY only** (`withStableParcelIds`, djb2-xor over rounded points), so the same parcel hashes identically before/after any mutable-field edit (labelOffset/active/locked/setbacks) and the union dedupes it by id; two genuinely-distinct parcels differ in points → distinct ids. Only fills a MISSING id (in-planner parcels keep their `uid()`), idempotent + reference-stable on already-migrated data. Exact-geometry id-less duplicates collapse to one, which **self-heals the phantom copies the bug already persisted** on the next load. No change needed in `SitePlanner.jsx` — parcels reaching React state now always carry an id, so the chip drag matches exactly one.
- **Verified here (sandbox):** 6 new unit tests in `test/siteModel.test.js` (backfill determinism · geometry-only stability across a labelOffset edit · distinct-geometry distinct ids · existing id never rewritten · the merge repro now yields 1 not 2 · exact-dup self-heal) · full suite **2,788 green** · lint 0 errors · build green.
- **Verified here (headless, logged-out):** seeded a site with 3 id-less parcels (2 exact-geometry dupes, one carrying a dragged `labelOffset`, + 1 distinct), opened it in the real plan canvas → exactly **2** acre chips render (dupe collapsed, distinct survived), zero page errors. (Temp spec, removed after the run — the unit tests are the durable guard.)
- **⏳ V225** = the signed-in / cloud pass: on a real account whose project has (or is seeded with) id-less parcels, drag an acreage label repeatedly across cloud syncs / a second tab and confirm it stays put with NO new copies, and that any pre-existing phantom copies collapse on load.

### B667 — Review remembers the last document PER PROJECT (+ the resume self-clobber fix) `[Doc Review]` (feature + bug — owner request) #doc-review #persistence  *(owner chat 2026-07-05 — "whatever I last reviewed, what the last document that I reviewed in that project should stay open too"; **B667** = B666 + 1. Branch `claude/module-nav-project-persistence-ryftwj`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED this session; parks in ⏳ Verify (Verify: live — resume needs signed-in cloud loads; timing class) → V217.**
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-05 from chat
- **AUDIT-FIRST find — resume was self-clobbering (the real reason Review "started from nothing"):** the mount-time pointer writes (`lastSingleId` = this session's fresh blank id, `lastMode`="review") ran in declaration order BEFORE the boot effect read the keys back, so resume loaded a never-saved review and silently fell to the empty state on every reload. Same pattern in `Stitcher.jsx` (`lastStitchId`). Fixed structurally: the stored pointers are captured at FIRST RENDER (before any effect can write) and all pointer writes stay silent until boot resolves — no clobber window at all.
- **Per-project memory:** new map `planyr:docreview:lastDoc:v1` = `{ [projectId|""]: {id, mode} }` (`lib/lastDoc.js` — pure, 14 unit tests). Legacy globals keep being written and remain the fallback (migration = fallback, not a copy pass — existing devices resume day one). Boot resolves ordered candidates via `resolveResume` (URL project → that project's own entry first, then legacy, still guarded by `wrongProject` on the actually-loaded record — a project-matched entry now RESUMES where the guard used to drop to empty). Breadcrumb project switch inside Review lands on THAT project's last doc (flushes the outgoing doc first; a pending cross-workspace open intent or an in-flight open wins — no race).
- **DEDUPE-FIRST:** no prior per-project-resume item (grepped `lastSingleId` · `resume` · `wrongProject`); B478 (resume-into-planner) is the Site-side analogue, different surface.
- **Verified here (sandbox):** `test/lastDoc.test.js` 14 green · full suite green · build green.
- **⏳ V217** = signed-in: open doc X in project A and doc Y in project B → breadcrumb A↔B resumes each project's own doc; reload a deep link `#/project/A/markup` reopens X; reload with an empty hash reopens the exact doc last on screen (also covers the B666 module+project restore chain end-to-end).

- **Verified here (sandbox headless):** `npm run build` green + `ui-audit/verify-landing.mjs` (desktop/tablet/phone, 8 scroll stops each) — `__landingReady` true, 0 page errors, new hero renders. **⏳ V212** = the live planyr.io/landing/ check after the Cloudflare deploy (stale-cache risk is exactly why this is `Verify: live`).

### B651 — Parcel split double-counts acreage; make split REPLACE the parent (parent + children can never both be active) `[Site Planner]` (bug) #site-planner #yield #selection  *(owner brief 2026-07-04, arrived as "NEW-1"; **B651** = highest real B# across both files (B650) + 1. Branch `claude/parcel-split-double-count-vk8f0j`. DEDUPE-FIRST — net-new: NOT B416 (Split-a-parcel discoverability / panel reachability, Done), NOT B128 (concave-cut split GEOMETRY, Done). Same feature area, different defect: those made the split tool reachable and its cut correct; this fixes what the split does to the parcel MODEL / active set.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + headless-verified this session; parks in ⏳ Verify (Verify: live — repro cites real project data) → V210.** A split parcel and its children occupy the SAME ground, so any active set containing a parent AND a child double-counts that acreage (owner repro: Parcel 3, 16.40 ac → 2.52 + 13.87 ac children, all three active → Yield sums ≈ 31.8 ac).
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-04 from chat
- **AUDIT-FIRST reconciliation (code reality vs. the report):** the current `performSplit` (`SitePlanner.jsx`, since PR #444 / #468) already **replaced + tombstoned** the parent, so the exact "split tool leaves all three active" no longer reproduces via the cut tool on `main`. The owner's live ≈31.8 ac most plausibly came from **overlapping county parcels added separately** (a recently-subdivided tract where CAD still lists the parent + both children) or a **stale cached bundle** predating that fix — which is exactly why **B652 (the overlap warning) is the real catch-all** and was built alongside. This item still had a genuine gap vs. the owner's desired UX (the old code DELETED the parent instead of retaining it), so the split was re-architected from "delete parent" to "supersede parent."
- **What shipped (branch `claude/parcel-split-double-count-vk8f0j`; lint 0 · 2,526 tests (+21) · build green · lazy split intact · headless `ui-audit/verify-b651-b652-parcel-split.mjs` 14/14):**
  - **Split is now a REPLACEMENT via supersession** (`performSplit`): one op creates + activates the pieces as CHILDREN (each carries `parentId`) and marks the parent `active:false` (superseded, non-counting) — no longer deleted/tombstoned. Because the superseded parent is inactive, it drops out of every active-parcel area sum automatically (no yield-math change needed; the ~13 inline `active !== false` sums are untouched).
  - **Parent retained + nested** (`parcelOutline` in `siteModel.js`; Parcel panel): the superseded parent stays in the list, greyed + "· split", with its children indented under it. The **on-canvas** superseded outline is hidden (its active children occupy the same ground). Header "Parcels · N" counts CURRENT lots only (excludes superseded), so splitting one lot reads "Parcels · 2".
  - **Lineage naming** (`parcelDisplayInfo`, derived — not stored): Parcel 3 → 3A / 3B → 3A1 / 3A2 (letters odd depth, digits even), tracking the parent's current number; a street address still wins as the name.
  - **Mutual-exclusion guard** (`toggleParcelActive` + `lineageConflicts`): activating a parcel auto-deactivates its ancestors AND descendants (a parent covers its children's ground; siblings are disjoint), so a parent and its split children can never both be active.
  - **Schema:** `SITE_MODEL_VERSION` 10 → 11 (additive `parentId`; existing records migrate losslessly — missing = root, unchanged behavior). Fixtures/MAP regenerated.
- **⏳ V210 (live, signed-in + real project data):** on planyr.io, load a real project, split a real county parcel (e.g. Parcel 3, 16.40 ac); confirm Yield reads ~16.4 ac (not ~31.8), the parent shows greyed "· split" with 3A/3B nested, toggling the parent active deactivates the children, and the whole thing round-trips through cloud save/reload without resurrecting the parent as active. (The pure model + logged-out UI are headless-verified; the signed-in cloud path + owner-data repro are the remaining live gate.)

### B659 — Sheet reader + file organizer revamp: rotated/offset pages, set-aware titles, left-edge & vertical title blocks, title-first grouping, date-first names `[Doc Review / Library]` (bug — owner report "they both kinda suck… it always messes up in every file") #doc-review #library #files #filing  *(owner chat 2026-07-05 with a screenshot of the GPL Arch IFR review showing "GRAND PORT LOGISTICS" on nearly every rail row + "4 SHEETS · 44 PAGES"; **B659** = highest real B# across both files (B658) + 1 — renumbered from a provisional B653 on the origin/main merge-in: a concurrent owner-brief batch took B653–B658; code comments updated in the same commit. DEDUPE-FIRST — extends the B266/B348/B378/B412 reader line and the B180/B312 organizer line, but the root causes here (page /Rotate ignored, no cross-page signal, no left-edge/vertical title blocks, item-first grouping) are net-new. Branch `claude/sheet-reader-file-organizer-my485w`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + verified against the owner's REAL Drive sets this session; parks in ⏳ Verify (Verify: live — repro cites real project data) → V213.** Every file misread because of five compounding engine gaps; all five are fixed and the fix is retroactive (rail meta is recomputed on every open — nothing cached to invalidate).
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-05 from chat
- **Root causes found (AUDIT-FIRST, against 6 real sets downloaded from the owner's Drive — GPL, Jacintoport, Mesa ×3, Goose Creek ALTA):**
  1. **Page rotation/origin ignored** — `extractPageItems` read raw PDF text coordinates, but the owner's real files are stored rotated (GPL **180°**, Mesa mech/site + GC ALTA **270°**) or origin-shifted (Jacintoport MediaBox at −1296,−864), so every zone/band/title/number read looked at the wrong part of the page. Now every run is mapped through the **viewport transform** (what a human sees), any rotation/origin.
  2. **No cross-page signal** — the title block prints the PROJECT NAME/client/architect stamps LARGER than the sheet title, so the per-page "tallest line" pick returned "GRAND PORT LOGISTICS" on every sheet. New pure module `src/shared/files/sheetTitleSet.js`: per-page ranked `titleCandidates` + a set-level pass (`refineSheetTitles`) that demotes candidates repeating across ≥45% of pages (identity stamps) unless they carry a drawing-type word (tiled-run titles), and hard-drops the app's own KNOWN project names/aliases/addresses (`projectStopTexts`; wired in DocReview rail, Stitcher, via `readSheets({stopTexts})`).
  3. **Left-edge & vertical title blocks unreadable** — Powers Brown-style blocks (the GPL architect) put the number top-corner at 2× any type and run titles VERTICALLY. `detectTitleBlock` now knows **left** bands; `reconstructLines` reconstructs **rotated runs as columns** (true reading order, CCW bottom→top) and fuses **glyph-stacked** pseudo-vertical strings (the Mesa "O I C I 119641 T E" gibberish → real lines); wrapped multi-line titles join (incl. across interleaved small cells); a spatial **label-anchored number read** takes the code item NEAREST a "SHEET NUMBER/SHEET NO./DWG NO." caption (content-order joins read the plot timestamp "6/23/2026" as sheet "6"); whole-page prominent-code last resort (≥1.5× everything else) for blocks that print the number outside every strip.
  4. **Identity/stamp rows could win as titles** — new rejections: firm rows (INC/LLC/…ARCHITECTS/…ENGINEERING/…PLATTING endings), phones/web/email, "Suite N"/street addresses/city-state-zip/lone-state cells, TBPE/TBPLS registrations, "(A) PROJECT FOR …"/"PREPARED FOR …", the TX interim-review stamp ("PRELIMINARY — NOT FOR CONSTRUCTION… / CURRENT AS OF…"), data-field rows ("SITE AREA : 29.17 AC"), textual dates, mostly-single-letter shreds, and a leading glued sheet-code ("C-2 TOPO SURVEY I" → "TOPO SURVEY I").
  5. **Item-first grouping collapsed distinct sheets** — 44 arch pages sharing item "Architectural" with consecutive numbers became "4 SHEETS". `groupKey` is now **title-first** (with `tileBaseTitle` stripping trailing tile counters "III"/"AREA 2"/"(1 OF 4)" so real tiles still chain); the coarse item is only the no-title fallback; rail/tray labels (`displayTitle`) now show the sheet's OWN title.
- **Organizer half (Library):** list sorts by the DOCUMENT's date (`docRecency` — issue/revision date first, upload time tiebreak; "latest revision on top" was a lie under updatedAt-sorting), auto-names are **date-first** matching the owner's own convention (`composeTitle`/server `composeFiledName` → "2026.06.20 Katy Grand - Grading Plan"), rows show the captured **sheet number/range badge** (toFileFact now carries sheet_number/sheet_title), and a typed re-file discipline normalizes case-insensitively onto the canonical DISCIPLINES list (no more typo-minted duplicate subcategory nodes).
- **Verified in-sandbox:** corpus harness over the 6 real Drive sets — GPL reads "WALL SECTIONS AND DETAILS · A303–A306" + "FIRE MARSHAL · FM101" (was "GRAND PORT LOGISTICS" ×5, no numbers); Jacintoport 10/11 real titles + all numbers (was "SPEC OFFICE" stamps); Mesa mech full titles + numbers M101-A–M303-A (was single-letter gibberish, no numbers); GC ALTA full survey title ×4 (was "PLATTING"). Full suite 2,568 tests green (44 new across sheetTitleSet/sheetMeta/sheetGroups/fileFacts/docFiling); headless rail check on the real GPL split PDF (V213 sandbox half).
- **Known residuals (minor, logged honestly):** scanned/no-text sets (Mesa electrical) still show "Sheet N" until the B364 OCR path; a form-style cover (Jacintoport S-1 county checklist) can read a checklist heading as its title; 2 of 11 Jacintoport titles are partial fragments ("AND NOTES"-class) when a 3-line title defeats the join; the curated Folders tree (B650) and auto-filed flat Drive paths remain two disconnected taxonomies — that unification belongs to the open **B650** umbrella, not here.
- **⏳ V213 (live, signed-in):** see `VERIFICATION.md` V213 — reopen the owner's saved "2026.06.23 GPL - Arch IFR" review on planyr.io and confirm per-sheet rail titles + sane sheet count; spot-check Library date-first names, doc-date sort, and the sheet-number badge on a fresh drop.
### B644 — Scheduler embed: first COLD boot throws `Cannot read properties of null (reading 'projects')` + the loader overlay exceeds the 6s backstop (self-recovers) (×2) `[Scheduler / robustness]` (bug — first-paint hardening) #scheduler  *(Cowork live verification 2026-07-03, from V153; minted **B644** = highest real B# across both files (B643) + 1)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + headless-verified 2026-07-05; parks in ⏳ Verify (Verify: live — timing/race class) → V211.** Original report: the FIRST cold Site→Schedule switch on planyr.io threw a one-time `⚠️ This view failed to load — Cannot read properties of null (reading 'projects')` (~10.5s overlay, self-recovered on re-nav).
- Verify: live
- Recurrence: 2026-07-05 — owner repro (chat "NEW-5", DEDUPE-FIRST fold — same error string, same first-paint null-`projects` read): create a project via **Start blank → Schedule tab** → the same error renders **behind the connect-a-schedule modal**. Deterministic (not only the cold race); expected a clean empty state only.
- **Root cause (pinned by a live sandbox repro, not a guess):** NOT the render path — the `if (!data) return <loader/>` gate was already sound. The **shell→iframe nav bridge** (`planar:nav-select` / `nav-select-by-site` / `nav-link` / `nav-create-linked` / `nav-dashboard` / `nav-new` / rename / delete in `public/sequence/index.html`) queues `setData(d => …)` functional updaters when the shell announces the active project on a tab switch; before the async `hs-v1` load resolves `d` is **null**, and React runs the queued updater INSIDE the next `useState` mount — `Object.values(d.projects || {})` throws and lands App in the error boundary. Cold boot = the race version (the bridge message beats the slow cloud load); fresh project = the deterministic version (no schedule linked, load still pending). Captured stack: updater → `Object.useState` → `App`. The prior "sandbox can't boot the embed" blocker is stale — the repro serves the embed's CDN deps from local copies via request interception (see the harness).
- **Fix shipped (minimal, matches the in-file `planar:view-set` precedent):** one early gate in the nav-bridge handler — drop `planar-shell` messages until `latestData.current` exists (the shell re-posts nav intents on every tab switch and retries `nav-request`, so an early drop self-heals the moment the load lands — the already-documented pre-load no-op behavior, now applied to every branch) — plus null guards in the three bridge-called helpers (`addProject` / `renameProject` / `deleteProject`) so a future caller can't regress the class.
- **Sandbox-verified 2026-07-05:** `ui-audit/verify-b644-fresh-null.mjs` (new, self-contained — fetches the four CDN deps once via curl, serves them by request interception): pre-fix it reproduces the exact owner error + stack; post-fix it PASSES (embed renders, zero null-`projects` errors). `jsxcheck-sequence` OK · build green.

### B672 (×2) — Element-level sync, phase 3/5: realtime read path + rejoin refetch (read cutover; blob frozen) `[Site Planner]` (feature) #site-planner #persistence  *(owner brief 2026-07-06, arrived as "NEW-3"; minted **B672** — see B671's renumber note. Branch `claude/site-elements-schema-sync-4p2x5b`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED this session; parks in ⏳ Verify (Verify: live — cross-tab propagation is a multi-session timing class) → V229.** Each open site now subscribes to its `site_elements` rows and applies changes LIVE; with the edit lock still on, a read-only tab updates in real time. This is also the READ CUTOVER: signed-in loads come from rows + a slim header, and the whole-doc blob is FROZEN (`sites.data_backup` = the ~30-day rollback copy).
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-06 from chat
- **Recurrence (2026-07-07, from the Cowork V229 live run — re-opened, FIXED same session, back to ⏳ Verify):**
  **V229 #5 FAILED with a reproduced LOST UPDATE (data-loss class).** Repro: session B's realtime socket
  dropped (`pfSupabase.realtime.disconnect()`), A edits an element (rev 9→10), B rejoins → the DB ends up
  clobbered back to B's stale geometry at rev 11; reproduced twice. **Root cause — the refetch-replace
  stale-reconcile race:** after `eng.seed(freshRows)` the old `refetchReplace` reconciled against
  `stateRef.current`, which still holds the PRE-replace canvas (setState hadn't rendered) — on a
  socket-dropped tab that canvas is genuinely stale, so the diff committed OLD geometry as valid
  rev-guarded updates on top of the fresh revs. (#4 passed because a hidden tab still receives events;
  only a dropped socket leaves the canvas stale.) Compounding hole: `flush()` clears the dirty map
  up-front, so the batch IN FLIGHT was invisible to both `applyRemoteRow` and the refetch substitution.
  **Fix (this session):** `refetchReplace` now reconciles against EXACTLY the substituted collections it
  just placed (rows ∪ pending local edits), never `stateRef`; it defers wholesale while `busyRef` is live;
  the engine tracks `inflightKeys` during a flush — in-flight commits are protected like dirty everywhere
  (`applyRemoteRow` keeps local + adopts rev; `dirtyEntries()` includes them so the refetch substitution
  keeps a mid-commit edit; `reconcile` skips re-enqueueing data already on the wire; shadow revs stay
  monotonic when an ok result lands after a newer remote rev was adopted; an identical incoming row is
  adopted silently and drops a duplicate queued write). 6 new unit tests pin the exact #5 sequence +
  in-flight invariants (`test/elementSync.test.js`, "refetch-replace safety"). **Re-run V229 #5 live with
  true DevTools offline** (the Cowork run's disconnect() only severed realtime, not the RPC path — DevTools
  offline exercises the queued-commit + rejoin path end-to-end).
  - *Watch note (Observation B, same run):* two transient paint freezes were seen under automation-driven
    load; nothing reproduced organically. No action — watch during the V229 re-run; escalate to its own B#
    only if it shows up under human use.
  - *Related churn fixed same session (Observation A):* the autosave pushed a content-identical slim header
    on every element edit — each push bumped `sites.version` and CAS-ping-ponged every other tab (a heal per
    edit; noise, and it masked #5's mechanism). `cloudUpsert` now skips a push whose header content is
    unchanged (`headerSig` — the slim header minus `updatedAt`; baseline seeded from `cloudList`, advanced on
    every successful push, cleared on delete/user-switch; the unload keepalive shares the skip). Trade-off,
    accepted: `sites.updated_at` advances only on REAL header changes (meta/settings/overlays) — element
    recency lives on the `site_elements` rows. +3 headerSig tests in `test/headerSlim.test.js`.
- **Realtime read path:** one channel per open site (`postgres_changes` filtered to `site_id`); the apply is idempotent per row (`applyRemoteRow`: incoming.rev must BEAT the shadow rev, so our own committed echoes are no-ops); a tombstoned row removes the element; a row for a locally-dirty element keeps LOCAL data and adopts the remote rev (its commit re-targets the fresh row). Remote applies buffer mid-gesture (never yank the canvas mid-drag). **Full refetch + REPLACE on every join/rejoin + tab wake** (visibilitychange) — never trust event gaps; dirty entries substitute back in; value-identical replaces keep state references (an idle wake re-trues nothing, saves nothing). A failed refetch changes nothing and retries (B54 discipline). No-realtime fallback: a plain fetch still seeds + replaces once, so writes work even if WebSockets are blocked.
- **Header slimming (same commit):** `slimForCloud` strips the 5 vector collections + marks `elementsInRows: true`; `mergePulledSites` understands slim rows (local elements kept — empty ≠ deleted; header-only re-push signature — no perma-push; a slim row's stale `deletedIds` are excluded from the union so they can never drop a row-restored element).
- **Kill list executed:** the B459 thin-clobber guard + `siteContent`/`siteTombs` baselines + `noteLocalContent` (a slim header would always read as "thinned"; element safety now lives in per-row rev guards); doc-level `cloudConflict` state + the blocking "changed in another session … Take over editing" banner (a stale header CAS now SELF-HEALS inside `cloudUpsert` — refetch the version, re-push once; the B455/B460/B558/B596 false-conflict class is retired BY ARCHITECTURE); the cloud-active storage-event union fold (signed-out keeps it). `deletedIds` refinement: element ids are reconciled against live rows on every refetch (an id with a live row is purged — rows are deletion-canonical), and it keeps serving header-side collections + signed-out mode.
- **DB executed via Supabase MCP:** backfill re-run captured the phase-1→3 gap (els 496→523 — real owner edits); found + fixed a guard edge (the boot re-push can rewrite blob CONTENT, e.g. the v12 `z` normalization, without advancing `updatedAt` → the update guard is now `<=`, engine rows stay strictly newer and untouched); fidelity after heal: **27/28 sites byte-identical, 1 site's rows strictly AHEAD of its blob** (rev 19, server-stamped 400ms after the last blob snapshot — the healthy dual-write case, rows-canonical). `data_backup` frozen for all 28 sites (`db/site_elements_freeze.sql`).
- **e2e seeds** now explode fixture sites into rows (seed.sql + seed-fixtures.sql), so seeded fixtures open under the rows-canonical read path.
- **Verified here (sandbox):** lint 0 · 2,835 tests (+19: `elementApply` matrix incl. the composite-key twin case, `headerSlim` merge/no-perma-push/stale-tombstone cases; `cloudThinGuard.test.js` retired with its guard) · build green · headless smoke 3/3 (signed-out planner unaffected — engine + channel are cloud-active-only).
- **⏳ V229 (live, two signed-in sessions):** see VERIFICATION.md — cross-tab <2s propagation, rejoin refetch, tab-wake re-true, and the no-conflict-banner regression. Folded into the consolidated Cowork runbook (docs/COWORK-ELEMENT-SYNC-LIVE.md, lands with B674).
